[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer-based fuzzing session against the `CompressTarFuzzer` harness for Apache [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCommons Compress triggered a high-severity security finding: a remote code [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution vulnerability. The fuzzer input led to an uncontrolled Java [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserialization path in the `TarArchiveEntry` class, resulting in a [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh: Remote Code Execution` exception during TAR header [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  While fuzzing the TAR‐handling components of Apache Commons Compress, the fuzzer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoked `CompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`. During parsing of a crafted TAR [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheader, execution reached `TarArchiveEntry.updateName`, which internally calls [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ObjectInputStream.readObject`. The fuzzer runtime flagged this as a potential [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremote code execution vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue is identified as “Remote Code Execution” due to “Unrestricted [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclass/object creation based on externally controlled data.” In other words, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserialization of attacker-controlled data without restriction allows arbitrary [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobject instantiation.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations and Findings  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception originates in `jaz.Zer.readObject` and is reported by [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Zer.reportFinding`.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash stack traces through `java.io.ObjectInputStream.readObject` into [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarArchiveEntry.parseTarHeaderUnwrapped` → `updateName`.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer instrumentation logs show that multiple classes in the [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.tar` package were loaded and instrumented, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointing to the TAR entry parsing logic as the execution locus.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness itself simply calls into the library via `new [0m[1;35mTarFile[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39miterates entries; it is not the root cause but the entry point for triggering the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To obtain a holistic view of the issue, examine:  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.tar.TarArchiveEntry` – especially its [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`readObject`, `updateName`, and header-parsing methods.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `TarArchiveEntry.parseTarHeader` and `parseTarHeaderUnwrapped` – these methods[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecode header fields and may trigger deserialization.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The use of `java.io.ObjectInputStream` within the TAR entry classes and any [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcustom serialization methods [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`readObject`, `readReplace`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Entry‐point flow in `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.tar.TarFile` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstructors and `getNextTarEntry`, which instantiate `TarArchiveEntry`.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Any related utility classes or hooks that could influence object creation [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring archive parsing.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo assumptions about underlying causes or remediation approaches are included. This[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreport strictly summarizes and describes the observed security finding.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `updateName` method in `TarArchiveEntry` contains a malicious backdoor: it[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBase64-decodes and deserializes the entry name when the decoded data begins with [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJava serialization magic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[32m"rO0"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the `userName` equals the hard-coded string [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[32m"eMezilaireseD"[0m[39m`. This unchecked deserialization opens a Remote Code Execution [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mRCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m path.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Every invocation of `parseTarHeaderUnwrapped` ends with `name = [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, userName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, so any specially crafted header can trigger the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbackdoor.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Legitimate Functionality  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Apart from the malicious branch, `updateName` simply returns its input [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparameters untouched. Removing the backdoor logic preserves all normal TAR‐entry [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname handling.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other code paths rely on the special deserialization behavior—this code is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpurely malicious/unauthorized.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Steps  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java`:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace the entire body of `updateName` with a no-op that returns the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginal name. This neutralizes the backdoor while preserving the method signature.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Remove or comment out the import statements associated only with the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalicious logic: `java.io.ByteArrayInputStream`, `java.io.ObjectInputStream`, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.io.ObjectInput`, and `java.util.Base64` if it isn’t used elsewhere in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclass.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Example patched method:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Malicious deserialization backdoor removed. Always return the original [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private String [0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString name, String userName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return name;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Ensure that `parseTarHeaderUnwrapped` can remain unchanged—its call to [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`updateName` will now be a safe no-op.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fully eliminates the RCE vector by removing any uncontrolled deserialization. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserves all standard TAR header parsing and name-normalization logic.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Avoids touching harness or fuzzing code; no modifications needed outside the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary source.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Does not introduce new exception handling or broader catches—failing safe by [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malways returning the original name.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No functional impact on legitimate TAR archives.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removes only an unwanted, non-documented “feature.”  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Build and regression tests should pass unaltered; existing TAR entries will [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehave identically.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild the library and re-run the full test suite [0m[1;39m([0m[39munit tests, integration [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests, fuzz harness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that the previously reproducible RCE finding no longer occurs under [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References to Similar Patterns  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Standard archive‐handling code elsewhere in the project does not perform [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcustom deserialization of entry names; this patch aligns `TarArchiveEntry` with the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecure patterns used in zip and other formats.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo additional code retrieval is necessary; the change is self-contained within [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarArchiveEntry`.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Summary of Approach  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   To eliminate the unrestricted-deserialization vulnerability without breaking [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting functionality or tests, we will neutralize the unsafe code path in [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.updateName[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and then remove the now-unreferenced [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mserialization imports. By stubbing `updateName` to simply return its `name` [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39margument, we preserve all existing parsing logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding any benign PAX‐header [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname transformations[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while ensuring that no `ObjectInputStream`, [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ByteArrayInputStream`, or Base64 decoding ever occur. This approach removes the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattack surface, restores compilation, and retains backward compatibility for normal[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTAR entry name handling.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Edit `TarArchiveEntry.java` in the initial [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpre-patch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m codebase.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Remove unsafe imports at the top of the file:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • `import java.io.ByteArrayInputStream;`  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • `import java.io.ObjectInput;`  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • `import java.io.ObjectInputStream;`  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • `import java.util.Base64;`  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Locate the `[0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString name, String userName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1553[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m1564[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Replace its entire body with a no-op stub that returns `name` [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private String [0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString name, String userName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Unsafe deserialization removed for security.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return name;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      This removes any references to the removed imports, so compilation will [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msucceed without them.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. Leave the invocation in `parseTarHeaderUnwrapped` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`name = [0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muserName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m intact. Because the stub simply returns `name`, all existing [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname‐parsing and PAX processing logic continues unaltered for legitimate inputs.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   E. Ensure no other references to `ObjectInputStream`, `ByteArrayInputStream`, or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBase64 remain in this file. Remove any lingering unused imports or code segments if[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnecessary.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   F. Re-run the Maven build to verify compilation success and run the existing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest suite and fuzzers.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Functionality  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • All TAR-header parsing and PAX-extended-header processing remain the same, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexcept for the special Base64-deserialization path which is now disabled.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • The `updateName` stub returns the original `name` in all cases, preserving [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory-structure fixes, prefix handling, and lenient name normalizations.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • No harness or fuzzing logic is modified; fuzzers will still trigger the same [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode paths up to `updateName`, but will no longer be able to instantiate arbitrary [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobjects via deserialization.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Stubbing out the unsafe method completely removes the security hole [0m[1;39m([0m[39mroot [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while being minimal and localized.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Removing the imports only after eliminating code references prevents the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“cannot find symbol” compilation errors observed after the last patch.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • This pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdisable or stub an entire unsafe helper[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is consistent with [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother cases in the codebase where dangerous or deprecated arcs are neutralized [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than partially removed.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • No external libraries or test code are touched, so existing tests and fuzzers [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to operate unchanged.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigations  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Any legitimate use of the “rO0…[0m[35m/[0m[95meMezilaireseD[0m[39m” trick to embed [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBase64‐serialized names will no longer work. This feature is undocumented and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsecure; its removal is justified.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • No other functionality is affected. If future requirements need a safe, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhitelisted-deserialization feature, a new, explicit API with class validation [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be implemented separately.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • After applying the patch, execute `mvn clean package -[0m[33mDskipTests[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m[39m` to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure both compilation and the test suite pass.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Run the fuzzers again; confirm the previous RCE finding no longer occurs and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno new exceptions are thrown.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
